That should be an item of concern to all of us because it is not only food that can buy its way into the hands of someone sick--fat globules, bat guano--it also comes from those whose lives have been touched by tainted meat or poultry. Even the highest quality meat in the United States is probably tainted in one way or another.  To the extent that food safety needs to be looked at in this country, as it is done in Canada, is to overlook the success of the Paris agreement, which is currently in place
